   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |          1. Inputs - geometry, cross-section, edge length          |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

      1.1. Geometry
           * Geometric name                    : triangle_l2a
           * Geometric file type               : geo
           * The number of faces               : 1
           * The number of points              : 3
           * The number of edges               : 3

      1.2. Cross-section information
           * Section type                      : honeycomb lattice
           * The number of duplexes            : 2
           * The number of rows                : 1
           * The number of columns             : 2
           * Reference row                     : 1
           * Reference min/max column          : 1 / 2

      1.3. Edge length
           * The minimum edge length           : 42

      1.4. Design parameters
           * Junction modification             : opt
           * Vertex design                     : mitered vertex
           * Vertex modification               : const
           * Sticky-end for self connection    : off
           * Unpaired scffold nucleotides      : on
           * The number of bases in Tn         : depending on distance
           * Distance btw phosphate groups     : .420
           * Starting base pair ID             : 4
           * Axial rise distance [nm]          : .340
           * Radius of helix [nm]              : 1.000
           * The Gap between helixes           : .250
           * Angle of minor groove             : 150.000
           * Angle correction factor           : .000
           * Gap between two scaf xovers       : 3
           * Gap between xover(stap) and bound : 6
           * Gap between stap and scaf xovers  : 6
           * Gap between xover and first nick  : 10
           * Gap between xover and nick        : 3
           * Staple cutting method             : max
           * Non-circular stap by single xover : off
           * Minimum # of bases in scaf strand : infinite
           * Minimum # of bases in stap strand : 20
           * Midium # of bases in stap strand  : 40
           * Maximum # of bases in stap strand : 60
           * Scaffold sequence                 : M13mp18 sequence


   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |                2. Build modified edges and points                  |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

      2.1. Neighbor points from two faces sharing with the line
                   1 edge (  3->  2) | (Poi 1) -> left(+) :   1, right(-) :  -1, (Poi 2) -> left(+) :   1, right(-) :  -1
                   2 edge (  2->  1) | (Poi 1) -> left(+) :   3, right(-) :  -1, (Poi 2) -> left(+) :   3, right(-) :  -1
                   3 edge (  1->  3) | (Poi 1) -> left(+) :   2, right(-) :  -1, (Poi 2) -> left(+) :   2, right(-) :  -1

      2.2. Find neighboring edges from initial geometry
                   1 line, (point 1) -> left :    3, right :   -1, (point 2) -> left :    2, right :   -1
                   2 line, (point 1) -> left :    1, right :   -1, (point 2) -> left :    3, right :   -1
                   3 line, (point 1) -> left :    2, right :   -1, (point 2) -> left :    1, right :   -1

      2.3. Construct arm junction data
                   1 junc :    2-arms -> center point # :    1, lines # : (   2,    3)
                   2 junc :    2-arms -> center point # :    2, lines # : (   1,    2)
                   3 junc :    2-arms -> center point # :    3, lines # : (   1,    3)

      2.4. Set local coordinate system on initial edges
                   1 line : t1 -> [  1.00,  0.00,  0.00 ], t2 -> [  0.00,  0.00,  1.00 ], t3 -> [  0.00, -1.00,  0.00 ]
                   2 line : t1 -> [ -0.71,  0.71,  0.00 ], t2 -> [  0.00,  0.00,  1.00 ], t3 -> [  0.71,  0.71,  0.00 ]
                   3 line : t1 -> [  0.00, -1.00,  0.00 ], t2 -> [  0.00,  0.00,  1.00 ], t3 -> [ -1.00,  0.00,  0.00 ]

      2.5. Seperate edges from the vertex
           * The number of initial vertex   : 3
           * The number of initial edges    : 3
           * The number of seperated points : 6
           * The number of seperated lines  : 3

      2.6. Update junction data with the seperated points
                   1 junc :   2-arms -> seperated points - (   4,    5)
                   2 junc :   2-arms -> seperated points - (   2,    3)
                   3 junc :   2-arms -> seperated points - (   1,    6)

      2.7. Find the scale factor to adjust polyhedra size
           * The minumum edge length       : 42
           * Scale factor to adjust size   : 1.064

      2.8. Update edge length with the scale factor
                   1 edge -> edge length :   13.600 [nm] ->   41 BP, remaining length :    0.000 [nm]
                   2 edge -> edge length :   19.233 [nm] ->   58 BP, remaining length :    0.000 [nm]
                   3 edge -> edge length :   13.600 [nm] ->   41 BP, remaining length :    0.000 [nm]


   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |                 3. Build cross-sectional edges                     |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

      3.1. Cross-section information
           * Section type                   : honeycomb lattice
           * The number of duplexes         : 2
           * The number of rows             : 1
           * The number of columns          : 2
           * Reference row                  : 1
           * Reference min/max column       : 1 / 2
           * The number of modified points  : 6
           * The number of modified edges   : 3
           * The number of sectional points : 12
           * The number of sectional edges  : 6

      3.2. Update junctional data with cross-section infomation
                   1 junc, the number of arms :     2
                          Mod point # :     4 -> cross point # : (     4,    10 )
                          Mod point # :     5 -> cross point # : (     5,    11 )
                   2 junc, the number of arms :     2
                          Mod point # :     2 -> cross point # : (     2,     8 )
                          Mod point # :     3 -> cross point # : (     3,     9 )
                   3 junc, the number of arms :     2
                          Mod point # :     1 -> cross point # : (     1,     7 )
                          Mod point # :     6 -> cross point # : (     6,    12 )

      3.3. Generate cross-sectional geometry

      3.4. Update local vectors with the sectional ID


   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |                    4. Build the basepair model                     |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

      4.1. Pre-calculate the number of basepairs
           * The number of multiple points : 12
           * The number of multiple lines  : 6
           * The number of basepairs       : 280
           * The number of basepair conns  : 274

      4.2. Discretize multiple lines into basepairs
                   1 line ( 41-bp) - start node # :      1, end node # :     41, sec # :   0, init edge # :   1
                   2 line ( 58-bp) - start node # :     42, end node # :     99, sec # :   0, init edge # :   2
                   3 line ( 41-bp) - start node # :    100, end node # :    140, sec # :   0, init edge # :   3
                   4 line ( 41-bp) - start node # :    141, end node # :    181, sec # :   1, init edge # :   1
                   5 line ( 58-bp) - start node # :    182, end node # :    239, sec # :   1, init edge # :   2
                   6 line ( 41-bp) - start node # :    240, end node # :    280, sec # :   1, init edge # :   3

      4.3. Set connection for the junction
           * The number of junctions             : 3
           * The number of duplexes on each edge : 2

      4.4. Modify the length of duplex at the junction
           * Find the proper length of duplex at the junction
           * Update junction data with updated nodes
           * Detailed information on junction connectivity
                   1 junc -> # of nodes to be connected :       2
                            99 node -->     100 node,      type :    1
                           239 node -->     240 node,      type :    1
                   2 junc -> # of nodes to be connected :       2
                            41 node -->      42 node,      type :    1
                           181 node -->     182 node,      type :    1
                   3 junc -> # of nodes to be connected :       2
                             1 node -->     140 node,      type :    1
                           141 node -->     280 node,      type :    1

      4.5. Delete ghost node to avoid crash
           * The number of nodes before modfication : 358
           * The number of nodes after modfication  : 358

      4.6. Make sticky-end at 5'- end node near the junction
                   1 junc, # of arms :    2 --> Added node # :     100 ->    359, 
                   2 junc, # of arms :    2 --> Added node # : 
                   3 junc, # of arms :    2 --> Added node # :       1 ->    360, 
           * The number of newly added sticky bases : 2
           * The number of newly added elements     : 2
                   1 junc :  2-arms --> node # :      99    359 /////     312    296 ///// 
                   2 junc :  2-arms --> node # :      41     42 /////     344    328 ///// 
                   3 junc :  2-arms --> node # :     360    140 /////     351    358 ///// 

      4.7. The Edge length
           * The minimum edge length                : 42 bp
           * The maximum edge length                : 89 bp
           * # of edges that have different length  : 4
                +   42 bp edge length -> # :    2
                +   58 bp edge length -> # :    1
                +   64 bp edge length -> # :    2
                +   89 bp edge length -> # :    1

   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |              5. Build B-form DNA and scaffold route                |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

           * The number of initial bases in scaffold     : 360
           * The number of initial bases in stapple      : 360

           * Section type                                : honeycomb lattice
           * Starting base pair ID                       : 4

   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+
   |              8. Summary of DNA wireframe lattice                   |
   +--------------------------------------------------------------------+

      8.1. Geometry, cross-section and problem description
           * Full geometric name               : triangle_l2a_DX_42bp
           * The number of initial faces       : 1
           * The number of initial points      : 3
           * The number of initial edges       : 3
           * The number of modified points     : 6
           * The number of modified edges      : 3
           * The number of sectional points    : 12
           * The number of sectional edges     : 6
           * Section type                      : honeycomb lattice
           * The number of duplexes            : 2
           * The number of rows                : 1
           * The number of columns             : 2
           * Reference row                     : 1
           * Reference min/max column          : 1 / 2
           * The minimum edge-length           : 42bp
           * Junction modification             : opt
           * Constant edge length from mesh    : off
           * Gap between two scaf xovers       : 3
           * Gap between xover(stap) and bound : 6
           * Gap between stap and scaf xovers  : 6
           * Gap between xover and first nick  : 10
           * Gap between xover and nick        : 3
           * Maximum # of bases in scaf strand : infinite

      8.2. Scaffold routing and sequence design
